<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kinder.html>kinder</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">children</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kamer.html>kamer</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">room</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p>From <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kinderspullen.html>kinderspullen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">children's <a href = vnd.unilang:things.html>things</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

</p>

***kindertjes.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kindertjes.html>kindertjes</a> (17652)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Formed as the plural diminutive of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kinderen.html>kinderen</a></i>, the standard but irregular plural of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kind</a></i>, as if the latter <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> the regular plural of the (nonexistent) singular <i><a href = vnd.unilang:kinder.html>kinder</a></i>. The standard plural of the diminutive of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kind</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kindjes.html>kindjes</a></i>, but this alternative form <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> common.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kip.html>kip</a> (1696)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Possibly from an imitative birdcall, or related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*kiukīną</i> (compare <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kuiken.html>kuiken</a></i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kieken.html>kieken</a></i>).<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_6">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kip.html>kip</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kippen.html>kippen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kippetje.html>kippetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kipje.html>kipje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chiefly <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Netherlands" class="extiw" title="w:Netherlands">Netherlands</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A chicken, <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Gallus_gallus_domesticus" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Gallus gallus domesticus"><i>Gallus gallus domesticus</i></a></span>.</li>
<li>A female chicken, a <a href = vnd.unilang:hen.html>hen</a>.

<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:flik.html>flik</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">klabak</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:politieagent.html>politieagent</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:smeris.html>smeris</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wout.html>wout</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lao_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lao language">Lao</a></span> <i class="Laoo mention" lang="lo">ກີບ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="lo-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kīp</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***kipper.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kipper.html>kipper</a> (43577)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">cypera</i> "male salmon," perhaps related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">coper</i> "reddish-brown metal" (see copper), on resemblance of color. Another theory connects it to <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:kip.html>kip</a></span> "sharp, hooked lower jaw of the male salmon in breeding season," from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:kippen.html>kippen</a></i> "to seize, snatch" but OED doubts this.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:kipper.html>kipper</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">kippers</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A split, salted and smoked herring or salmon.</li>
<li>A male salmon after spawning.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military<span class="ib-comma">,</span> RAF World War II code name</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A patrol to protect fishing <a href = vnd.unilang:boats.html>boats</a> in the Irish and North <a href = vnd.unilang:seas.html>Seas</a> against attack from the air.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> naval <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <a href = vnd.unilang:torpedo.html>torpedo</a>.
<ul><li><b>2009</b>, Jean Hood, <i>Submarine</i> (page 197)
<dl><dd>'Fancy running the risk of getting a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:kipper.html>kipper</a></b> [a <a href = vnd.unilang:torpedo.html>torpedo</a>] to go with his <a href = vnd.unilang:grub.html>grub</a>.'</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:kipper.html>kipper</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">kippers</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">kippering</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">kippered</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">cooking</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To prepare (a herring or similar fish) by splitting, salting, and smoking.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1836</b> March – <b>1837</b> October<b> | </b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Charles_Dickens" class="extiw" title="w:Charles Dickens">Charles Dickens</a>,  chapter 49, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Pickwick_Papers" class="extiw" title="w:The Pickwick Papers">The Posthumous Papers of the Pickwick Club</a></cite>, London |  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chapman_%26_Hall" class="extiw" title="w:Chapman amp; Hall">Chapman and Hall</a>,<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="186, Strand">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span>, published 1837, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/28228280">28228280</a></small>:</span><dl><dd></dd></dl></div>
<dl><dd>There <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <b>kippered</b> salmon, and Finnan haddocks, and a lamb's head, and a haggis<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Short form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">UKIP</i>  + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>, influenced by <i><a href = vnd.unilang:kipper.html>kipper</a></i>, the type of fish.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:kipper.html>kipper</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">kippers</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> humorous<span class="ib-comma">,</span> often with capital</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A member or supporter of UKIP (UK Independence Party).</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps akin to Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">kjapt</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">briskly; impetuously</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">kippa</i> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">"to snatch; pull; jerk" gt; Middle English <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:kippen.html>kippen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to seize</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">kipra</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to wrinkle; draw tightly</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, Norwegian <i class="Latn mention" lang="no">kjapp</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fast; brisk</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kippen.html>kippen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to seize; catch; <a href = vnd.unilang:grip.html>grip</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. More at <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:kip.html>kip</a></span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***kist.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kist.html>kist</a> (2180)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:kisten.html>kiste</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*kistō</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">cista</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">κίστη</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kístē</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*kisteh₂</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kist.html>kist</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kisten.html>kisten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kistje.html>kistje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>box, chest</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a <a href = vnd.unilang:boot.html>boot</a> or large shoe, especially an army <a href = vnd.unilang:boot.html>boot</a></li>
<li>coffin
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:doodskist.html>doodskist</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">lijkkist</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">aviation</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> aeroplane</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:kist.html>kist</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>/<span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>

***kitsch.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kitsch.html>kitsch</a> (43576)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:kitsch.html>Kitsch</a></i>, from dialectal <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">kitschen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to coat, to smear</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, the word and concept <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> popularized in the 1930s by several critics who contrasted it with <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/avant_garde" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:avant garde">avant <a href = vnd.unilang:garde.html>garde</a></a> art.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:kitsch.html>kitsch</a></strong> (<i>usually uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">kitsches</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Art, decorative <a href = vnd.unilang:objects.html>objects</a> and other forms of representation of questionable artistic or aesthetic value; a representation that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> excessively sentimental, overdone, or vulgar.
<ul><li><b>1939</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Clement_Greenberg" class="extiw" title="w:Clement Greenberg">Clement Greenberg</a>, "<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.sharecom.ca/greenberg/kitsch.html">Avant <a href = vnd.unilang:garde.html>Garde</a> and <a href = vnd.unilang:kitsch.html>Kitsch</a></a>", <i>The Partisan Review</i>,
<dl><dd>Because it can be <a href = vnd.unilang:turned.html>turned</a> out mechanically, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:kitsch.html>kitsch</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> become an integral part of our productive system in a way in which true culture could never be, except accidentally.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">camp</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:kitsch.html>kitsch</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">kitscher</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">more <a href = vnd.unilang:kitsch.html>kitsch</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">kitschest</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">most <a href = vnd.unilang:kitsch.html>kitsch</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Of art and <a href = vnd.unilang:decor.html>decor</a>: of questionable aesthetic value; excessively sentimental, overdone or vulgar.
<ul><li><b>1989</b>, Graham Greene, <i>Yours etc: <a href = vnd.unilang:letters.html>Letters</a> to the Press 1945-1989</i>, →ISBN, p. 243,
<dl><dd><span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span> a picture of lemur-eyed children of the sort one <a href = vnd.unilang:sees.html>sees</a> in the <b>kitscher</b> sort of Italian <a href = vnd.unilang:restaurant.html>restaurant</a> <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1996</b>, Robert Silberman, "The stuff of art: Judy Onofrio", <i>American Craft</i>, Jun/Jul 1996, pp. 40-45,
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:abe.html>Abe</a> Lincoln, Paul Bunyan and <b><a href = vnd.unilang:kitsch.html>kitsch</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:souvenir.html>souvenir</a> coconut heads come across as icons of masculinity.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2005</b>, Ronald Frame, "Critical <a href = vnd.unilang:paranoia.html>Paranoia</a>", <i>Michigan Quarterly Review</i>, Spring 2005, p. 285,
<dl><dd>I recognized her at once <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> though she wasn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> wearing the <a href = vnd.unilang:tweed.html>tweed</a> hunting outfit and the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:kitsch.html>kitsch</a></b> headwear.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Although the forms <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">kitscher</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">kitschest</i> are attested, those formed on <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">kitschy</i> are more common, particularly for the comparative.</li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kitty.html>kitty</a> (6209)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A kitten or young cat.</li>

<ul><li><b>2007</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:pam.html>Pam</a> Johnson-Bennett, <i>Starting from Scratch: How to Correct Behavior Problems in Your <a href = vnd.unilang:adult.html>Adult</a> Cat</i>
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>Even</a> how a child picks up and handles the cat can make the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:kitty.html>kitty</a></b> begin to fear the very sight of the youngster.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>A money pool, as for a card game, or for shared expenses.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">poker<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> In a home game, a small, specified amount <a href = vnd.unilang:taken.html>taken</a> from each <a href = vnd.unilang:pot.html>pot</a> to pay the host's expenses.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> vulgar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Female genitals. <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">Euphemistic form of <i>pussy</i>.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">card games</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A set of additional cards <a href = vnd.unilang:dealt.html>dealt</a> face down in some games.</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:klaarkomen.html>klaarkomen</a> (8888)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klaar.html>klaar</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ready</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:komen.html>komen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to come</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare to and distinguish neatly from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">klarkommen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to manage, to get by</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klaarkomen.html>klaarkomen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to get ready; to finish a task, to be finished
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:deze.html>Deze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:brug.html>brug</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vorige.html>vorige</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:maand.html>maand</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eindelijk.html>eindelijk</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:klaargekomen.html>klaargekomen</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">This bridge finally <b>reached completion</b> last month.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to come, to reach orgasm</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">clager</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">accuser, plaintiff</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. ***klant.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:klant.html>klant</a> (1786)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">calant</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">person, friend</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norman" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norman">Old Northern French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">calant</i> (compare regular Old French <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">chalant</i>), from <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">chaloir</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to heat, to care about</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">calēre</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to be hot</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klant.html>klant</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klanten.html>klanten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klantje.html>klantje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">klante</b>)

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">clap</i>.
